<h1 class="firstHeading mw-first-heading" id="firstHeading"><span class="mw-page-title-main">Library</span></h1>
<div class="vector-body" id="bodyContent">
<div class="noprint" id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
<div id="contentSub"><div class="flaggedrevs_short flaggedrevs_stable_synced plainlinks noprint" id="mw-fr-revisiontag"><div class="flaggedrevs_short_basic"><span class="flaggedrevs-icon oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-iconElement-icon oo-ui-icon-articleSearch oo-ui-iconElement oo-ui-labelElement-invisible oo-ui-iconWidget" title="Changes must be reviewed before being displayed on this page."></span><span class="fr-toggle-arrow oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-indicatorElement-indicator oo-ui-indicator-down oo-ui-indicatorElement oo-ui-labelElement-invisible oo-ui-indicatorWidget" id="mw-fr-revisiontoggle" title="show/hide details"></span></div>
<div id="mw-fr-revisiondetails-wrapper" style="position:relative;"><div class="flaggedrevs_short_details" id="mw-fr-revisiondetails" style="display:none">This is the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Pending_changes" title="Wikipedia:Pending changes">latest accepted revision</a>, <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;type=review&amp;page=Library">reviewed</a> on <i>1 October 2022</i>.</div>

<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">Jump to search</a>
<div class="mw-body-content mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">Organized collection of books or other information resources</div>
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1033289096">.mw-parser-output .hatnote{font-style:italic}.mw-parser-output div.hatnote{padding-left:1.6em;margin-bottom:0.5em}.mw-parser-output .hatnote i{font-style:normal}.mw-parser-output .hatnote+link+.hatnote{margin-top:-0.5em}</style><div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">For other uses, see <a class="mw-disambig" href="/wiki/Library_(disambiguation)" title="Library (disambiguation)">Library (disambiguation)</a>.</div>
<p class="mw-empty-elt">
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:332px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Statsbiblioteket_l%C3%A6sesalen-2.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3820" data-file-width="5165" decoding="async" height="244" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/Statsbiblioteket_l%C3%A6sesalen-2.jpg/330px-Statsbiblioteket_l%C3%A6sesalen-2.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/Statsbiblioteket_l%C3%A6sesalen-2.jpg/495px-Statsbiblioteket_l%C3%A6sesalen-2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/Statsbiblioteket_l%C3%A6sesalen-2.jpg/660px-Statsbiblioteket_l%C3%A6sesalen-2.jpg 2x" width="330"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Statsbiblioteket_l%C3%A6sesalen-2.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>A modern reading room in the <a href="/wiki/State_and_University_Library,_Denmark" title="State and University Library, Denmark">State and University Library, Denmark</a></div></div></div>
<p>A <b>library</b> is a collection of <a href="/wiki/Document" title="Document">materials</a>, books or media that are accessible for use and not just for display purposes. A library provides physical (hard copies) or <a href="/wiki/Electronic_media" title="Electronic media">digital access</a> (soft copies) materials, and may be a physical location or a virtual space, or both. A library's collection can include <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Printed" title="Printed">printed</a> materials and other physical resources in many formats such as <a href="/wiki/DVD" title="DVD">DVD</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/CD" title="CD">CD</a> and cassette as well as access to information, music or other content held on <a href="/wiki/Bibliographic_database" title="Bibliographic database">bibliographic databases</a>.
</p><p>A library, which may vary widely in size, may be organized for use and maintained by a public body such as a government; an institution such as a school or museum; a corporation; or a private individual. In addition to providing materials, libraries also provide the services of <a href="/wiki/Librarian" title="Librarian">librarians</a> who are trained and experts at finding, selecting, circulating and organizing information and at interpreting information needs, navigating and analyzing very large amounts of information with a variety of resources.
</p><p>Library buildings often provide quiet areas for studying, as well as common areas for group study and collaboration, and may provide public facilities for access to their electronic resources; for instance: computers and access to the <a href="/wiki/Internet" title="Internet">Internet</a>. The library's clientele and services offered vary depending on its type: users of a <a href="/wiki/Public_library" title="Public library">public library</a> have different needs from those of a <a href="/wiki/Special_library" title="Special library">special library</a> or academic library, for example. Libraries may also be community hubs, where programs are delivered and people engage in lifelong learning. Modern libraries extend their services beyond the physical walls of a building by providing material accessible by electronic means, including from home via the Internet.
</p><p>The services the library offers are variously described as library services, information services, or the combination "library and information services", although different institutions and sources define such terminology differently.
</p>
